        <div class="content">
         <header>
          <h3 class="article-name">
           Sony unveils new VR controllers for the PS5
          </h3>
          <p class="byline">
           <span class="by-author">
            By
            <span style="white-space:nowrap">
             What Hi-Fi?
            </span>
           </span>
           <time class="published-date relative-date" data-published-date="2021-03-19T14:54:10Z" datetime="2021-03-19T14:54:10Z">
           </time>
          </p>
         </header>
         <p class="synopsis">
          Sony has revealed its PS5 VR controllers, complete with adaptive triggers as seen on the PS5 DualSense.
         </p>
        </div>
       </article>
